< text>
Unfortunately after changing managers I had to change a once excellent review. Thai Time Bistro in Ocean Beach does not have consistency among chefs. Before the old chef took over as manager you could order any dish without fish sauce. Now you can only get those dishes without fish sauce when she is there. So vegan options are very limited. They also don't tell you there is fish sauce in things when you order a vegetarian option. You must inquire each visit, and ask if you can get it without the fish sauce. The manager told me any of the chefs can prepare the dish without fish sauce. But I have been told repeatedly by other wait staff that getting items without fish sauce is not an option for the chef that is cooking. I have spoken to them multiple times telling them cohesion is really important. But they basically told me that they are not catering to vegetarians or vegans. So I figured a shout out was important. I won't be eating there anymore. Unfortunately there isn't another Thai place in walking distance :(<//text>

< Text>
Awesome little town near the mountain, people are friendly and nice they will guide you even if you are lost in your life like me, but do get a map of the mountain and the open trails before venturing out and becoming eagle food. Please take water and fill up your gas near by. Unlike me Please listen to those people at the visitors center as they know what they talking they are not kidding when they say that altitude will make your brains hurt. Also ask them about the lake which is near the mountain. It's supposed to be very very beautiful and green with the snow capped mountain reflecting on the waters.

PS as bonus if you want to hike the whole mountain like I did please don't bother paying for permit as no one will be asking as there are no cops on top of the mountain asking for permits. And also for the permits you need a cheque(british for check), dont bother the hassle just enjoy the climb, high five some stonned hippies, they are in their natural habitat. Check the water fall I heard it's epic. I didn't had the time to see that because I was so busy battling my altitude sickness. Cheers!!< /Text>

<text>Update June 2020, Went in for the first time since the pandemic on June 24.  All the expected checks were done in advance with respect to the covid outbreak (temperature taken, questionnaire, stay in car not waiting room).  All the dental staff wear masks and face shields (during procedure) and there's a small suction cone that pulls the air directly from the region around your mouth while work is being done.  Everything went well and the staff were upbeat as always and I won't hesitate to go back under prevailing circumstances.
Dr. Fantino is at the top of her profession.  I've been a patient for several years and am on the older side with teeth that need a lot of attention (old fillings that need replacement, crowns).  Everything is done perfectly and it's a well managed practice where you're greeted when you enter the office and scheduled times are honored promptly.  Beyond cleanings additional procedures are only done when necessary since Dr. Fantino has noted that a specific tooth is giving high readings and it needs to be monitored in the future but for now the drilling can wait.  I can't say enough good things, this kind of confidence is hard to establish in a field like dentistry.< /text></record>

<rating>5< /rating>< text>
After thirty years of fruitless searching, I think that I've finally found The Perfect Dental Service.  Dr. Dyer's staff is remarkable: friendly, helpful, competent and willing to help in any way to make your visit as pleasant as possible.  The office is just plain beautiful -- instead of staring at a blank wall while having your teeth cleaned, you're treated to a panoramic view of a redwood and eucalyptus grove along Los Gatos Creek.  Office ambiance doesn't get much nicer than that.

Of course, the real treasure at Oak Meadow Dental Center is Dr. Dyer himself.  Apart from being a genuinely caring and personable individual, his technical expertise borders on wizardry.  The calm and confident way in which he performs his work thoroughly relieves any residual anxiety that you might feel about having dental repairs done, and as far as I can tell, the technology he employs is state-of-the-art in all ways.

Los Gatos is a little off the usual Silicon Valley beaten path, but it'll be very much worth the extra effort for you to visit Oak Meadow Dental Center.<//text>

<user>111397718843780056281< /user><response>None</response>< Review>
I've been attending since November 2018.  Love the workout (low impact).  I sometimes do two sessions in one day and also on back-to-back days with no problem (i had a previous hip injury that limited my running).

Staff is friendly and cordial.  The fellow rowers are also very amicable.  I can burn 700-800 calories in one session for the full row and I've lost about 10 pounds of weight in the last six weeks but i do go frequently.

The workout is not for everybody as it is very challenging and you need to find a way to push yourself throughout for max benefit.  Also, your hands can take a beating the first month or so and you may develop small calluses. My favorite classes are Full Row and House.  Bottomline, i think it is a great exercise and experience and I recommend to others.< /Review>

< Text>
I've been attending since November 2018.  Love the workout (low impact).  I sometimes do two sessions in one day and also on back-to-back days with no problem (i had a previous hip injury that limited my running).

Staff is friendly and cordial.  The fellow rowers are also very amicable.  I can burn 700-800 calories in one session for the full row and I've lost about 10 pounds of weight in the last six weeks but i do go frequently.

The workout is not for everybody as it is very challenging and you need to find a way to push yourself throughout for max benefit.  Also, your hands can take a beating the first month or so and you may develop small calluses. My favorite classes are Full Row and House.  Bottomline, i think it is a great exercise and experience and I recommend to others.</Text>

<Rate>5<//Rate>< review>
Green farm market has been providing nice fresh produce for many years. I went there to get some ingredients for beef pho and I went here, knowing it's a Vietnamese market or owned by one. I read reviews that the tidiness inside isn't the greatest, but I thought was okay. Anyways, it has a nice collection of fresh vegetables and vegetables. Price is generally very reasonable. Price is comparable to nearest El super, which offers great prices itself. Meat and fish departments closed earlier than 8:00pm when store closes. About the pho ingredients, I bought a variety of ethnic ingredients. Pho rice noodles, spices, seasonings, etc. Overall, nice friendly place with great priced grocery.< /review>

You would think that in this current times where there's a shopping panic and every store is low on stock that we, the shoppers, would be more understanding and empathetic to grocery stores like Green Farm.   While waiting in line, I chatted with some of the nice folks who worked there and they are all working non-stop to move the lines along as quickly as possible.  They are working tirelessly to do their best so the least we can do as shoppers, is have a little patience.  I shop here all the time and this is a rare situation with 10 times the customers and shortage of stock.  Don't go online and give a business a low rating because of this situation we are ALL in.</review>

I used to enjoy shopping at this market because it it located near my home.  This market carries a variety of ethnic produce; foods such as Jack-fruit, that I had never experienced before.
Sadly, I will never shop at this market again, as they have a policy that assumes that their customers are inherently thieves. The will take away your bag and give you a clothespin, which you can use to retrieve your bag after you have made your purchase.
